# Aira — 20 Full Reel Concepts · Set 5 (Concepts 71–90) · Sys Directive 3 v3.16-VP

Fully-detailed silent reel concepts (no voice — top-notch sound design only). New standing sections: Footwear, Accessories, Eye Colour (grouped near Wardrobe/Hair/Makeup). 6–8 frames per reel, up to 10 for a hero reel. Each concept unique vs. Sets 1–4.

---

# CONCEPT 71 — VERDANT CONSERVATORY / LIVING-VINE TOPIARY COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 5 — Verdant Botanical Luxe

Format: Transformation Reveal / Botanical Beauty Hero

Hero Product: "Flora" dew botanical face-oil — frosted emerald-glass bottle, gold leaf-embossed collar, luminous green-gold oil

Setting: Grand Victorian glass conservatory at golden-green morning light — towering topiary, climbing roses, tree ferns, mossy stone, drifting pollen-light

Wardrobe: moss-green silk-velvet column gown → living-vine topiary couture gown

Footwear: barely-there gold-leaf strappy heels, fine vine-wrapped ankle

Accessories: a single gold-leaf ear-climber + a fine emerald-drop pendant

Hair: Soft Botanical Updo with loose tendrils

Makeup: Dewy Garden-Fresh Glow

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference (warm hazel-brown); zero drift frame to frame

Movement: living-vine topiary growth wraps the gown → blossom-bloom burst

Concept Line: "she grows into bloom" (on-theme, NOT spoken)

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: LUSH · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centred botanical hero, deep conservatory depth

Grade: bright VIBRANT POP-COLOUR botanical — vivid emerald and moss green with electric pops of fuchsia, marigold, coral and electric-blue blossoms, gold-green daylight, dewy porcelain skin, high-saturation rich-but-open colour (pop-vivid, never muddy)

Spoken line: NONE — fully silent reel

Audio note: no voice on any frame; rich diegetic conservatory ambience + designed sound + a subtle Master Track Brief (present, never full-foreground)

Identity safety: AIRA identity placeholder every frame; adult, non-sexualized; eye colour locked to reference

Visual-lead note (silent reel): every beat carries on image + sound design alone — the living-vine transform and the blossom-bloom climax do the talking

Tonal-lane note: bright lush verdant/botanical lane — a fresh green departure from Set 4's gilded-ballroom, ink-atelier and crystal palettes

---

## Frame 1 of 6 — IMAGE PROMPT

IDENTITY LOCK: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here].

VISUAL-LEAD NOTE (silent reel): the opening sells place and poise on image alone — a luminous beauty stands amid a sunlit glass conservatory cradling the emerald oil; let the green-gold light, the dewy skin and the velvet gown establish the world with no dialogue.

WARDROBE: (start state) — a moss-green silk-velvet column gown, fully modest high neckline and long sleeve, the velvet pile catching the green-gold daylight as soft directional sheen bands; a clean princess seam, the hem pooling with real weight on mossy stone; fabric pristine, zero lint or stray threads.

FOOTWEAR: barely-there gold-leaf strappy heels, a slim 7cm heel, fine leaf-shaped gold straps crossing the foot, one delicate strand vine-wrapping the ankle; soft specular on the metallic leaf, real leather grain, matched to the gown, no mismatched footwear.

ACCESSORIES: a single slim gold-leaf ear-climber tracing the right ear, and a fine emerald-drop pendant resting at the hollow of the throat; both catching one clean pin-specular, understated and elegant, nothing competing with the hero product.

HAIR (Soft Botanical Updo): a soft low botanical updo with a gentle centre part, a few loose face-framing tendrils easing at the temple and nape, a natural soft sheen rather than a hard gloss; real strands with visible flyaway softness, hair colour locked to the reference.

MAKEUP (Dewy Garden-Fresh Glow): a dewy fresh base with lit cream highlight on the high cheekbone, brow-bone and cupid's bow; soft-brushed natural brows; a sheer rosewood-tint lip with a soft light-point; warm petal-pink blush on the apples; inner-corner brightener; skin kept dewy and real with visible pores and fine peach-fuzz (glow from light, never plastic).

EYE COLOUR: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; crisp twin daylight catchlights; zero colour drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia.

HANDS & NAILS: right hand cradling the frosted emerald bottle at collarbone height, fingertips light on the glass with natural nail-bed colour; left hand open and relaxed near a fern frond, fingers softly curved; almond nails in a clean rose-nude gloss, neat cuticles.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: a calm serene half-smile reaching the eyes, right brow lifted about 1mm, lips parted barely 1mm on a held breath, eyes direct to lens with bright catchlights; the faintest warmth at the cheeks; a slow settling blink mid-frame.

BODY POSTURE & WEIGHT: torso rotated about 5° to open the right shoulder to camera, weight settled on the back leg with a 2° hip counter-tilt, front shoulder dropped a touch, chin level, spine long; the stance alive and breathing, not posed-stiff (living stillness).

KINETIC STILLNESS (8 layers): (1) a loose tendril drifting at the temple in the conservatory air; (2) the green-gold oil rocking gently inside the tilted bottle; (3) drifting pollen-light motes floating slowly up-frame behind her; (4) a fern frond easing a few millimetres in the warm draught; (5) chest rising on a soft shallow inhale; (6) specular glints sliding along the curved emerald glass and gold collar; (7) the velvet pile shifting its highlight as her ribcage expands; (8) a slow eyelash settle completing a blink.

SPATIAL LOGIC: FOREGROUND — the frosted emerald bottle and cradling fingers at about 20% depth, tack sharp, label forward. MIDGROUND — Aira centred, three-quarter torso filling the frame. BACKGROUND — the grand glass conservatory receding deep: topiary, climbing roses, tree ferns, mossy stone, a sunlit glass roof, drifting pollen-light.

LIGHTING: KEY — soft green-gold morning daylight raking through the glass roof as a wrap beauty key. FILL — soft bounce off pale stone lifting under-chin shadow. RIM — a warm sun-rim skimming hair and shoulder for separation. PRACTICAL — sun shafts through the glass. SEPARATION — a brighter sunlit gap placed behind her head. BOUNCE — a hidden card adding a clean catch to the bottle glass.

FRAMING: ASPECT 9:16; medium close, chest-up, 12% headroom, the bottle entering the lower third, clean negative space camera-left to receive the transform.
SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: A medium-close chest-up framing with the subject filling roughly 55% of the vertical, about 12% headroom, the bottle in the lower third. Her body composed and near-frontal. Camera near at a chest-up distance, negative space camera-left in the verdant conservatory. Only head, shoulders and the product hand are in frame, the body near-frontal and centred. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 50mm, f/2.8; near eye and bottle label both crisp, the conservatory melting to creamy green bokeh, soft circular speculars off the glass roof; gentle highlight roll-off, no clipping.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: a luminous botanical beauty hero — product-at-face amid a sunlit conservatory, fresh, lush, phone-stopping.

ATMOSPHERE: fresh, serene, alive — dewy morning air, green growth and warm sun, the world about to bloom around her.

COLOR GRADE: bright verdant botanical — rich emerald and moss green, warm gold-green daylight, dewy porcelain skin, clean whites, blacks rich but open, full mid-tone detail, no teal-orange.

TEXTURE & MICRO-DETAIL: the frosted emerald glass shows a faint matte grain with a polished label window and a hairline condensation sheen; sub-surface glow through the green-gold oil; the gold leaf-collar throws a pin-sharp specular; real skin micro-texture with peach-fuzz catching rim light; a dew-bead trembling on a nearby leaf; one pollen mote drifting through the key beam.

SPOKEN LINE: NONE — silent opening; lips softly parted on a held breath, no speech.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, over-smoothed skin, oversharpened, AI artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, mismatched footwear, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, garbled label text, heterochromia, eye-colour drift.

## Frame 1 of 6 — VIDEO PROMPT

IDENTITY & CHARACTER-CONSISTENCY LOCK: render Aira strictly from the locked identity reference and hold her the SAME PERSON for the entire 6-second clip and every generated frame. Treat identity as a FIXED skeleton that never changes — bone structure (skull, cheekbones, jawline, chin), overall face shape and proportions, eye shape, spacing and iris colour, nose and lip shape, skin tone and real skin texture (visible pores, fine peach-fuzz; no plastic smoothing, no beautification creep, no face re-shaping), hairline, hair colour and texture, height, build and hand/finger anatomy. ONLY the soft expression muscles may move — eyelids, brows, cheeks and mouth corners — together with the eyes, gaze and head; expression and lip-sync animate ON TOP of that fixed identity and must NEVER alter the face shape, the eye colour, or who she is. Keep expression changes smooth and moderate and lead them with the EYES and GAZE (soft smiles, brow lifts, a parted breath, eyes tracing the object) — no extreme grimace, no wide-mouth distortion, no hard squint, no rapid expression flicker that would warp the geometry; favour one clean expression transition per clip. ABSOLUTE ZERO identity drift: no morphing, melting, smearing, rubbery warping, face-swapping, twinning or a second/duplicate subject, no age, weight, ethnicity or gender shift, no extra, missing or fused fingers or limbs. Identity stays identical at the first frame, every in-between frame, the loop seam and the last frame. Through any transform, impossible move or fast action ONLY the intended element (wardrobe, environment, props or effect) changes — her face, identity and proportions stay fully recognizable; interpolate strictly between the locked keyframes and never invent a new face, new hands, extra limbs or a second subject. Do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

SHOT TYPE: medium close, chest-up, subject fills about 55% of the vertical frame.

LENS: 50mm, f/2.8, creamy green fall-off.

SHOT BREAKDOWN (timed, 6s · real-time, continuous energetic motion — never slow-motion, never a static hold; expression eye-led and identity-safe):
- [00:00–00:02] Medium close chest-up: a slow push-in is already gliding toward her as she tilts the emerald oil bottle a few degrees into the sun, speculars sliding along the glass and the green-gold oil settling inside; gaze lowered to the glass.
- [00:02–00:04] The push continues as she lifts her eyes to lens on a soft inhale and a serene half-smile blooms, golden-green conservatory light warming her face.
- [00:04–00:06] She holds, calm and luminous, a loose tendril drifting at her temple, eyes soft and direct.

LIGHTING: soft green-gold daylight key with stone bounce fill; live moving speculars across glass and skin as the bottle tips; warm sun-rim steady on hair.

ENVIRONMENT: sunlit glass conservatory, topiary and ferns behind, drifting pollen-light.

AUDIO: diegetic-plus-design, no spoken word (silent reel). Ambient bed — a warm conservatory tone: distant birdsong, a soft draught through leaves, low. SFX — a soft glass-tap as fingers settle at 0.5s, a faint velvet shift at 2.5s, a delicate airy sparkle-shimmer at 3.8s timed to the eye-lift. Reaction — a soft audible breath at 2.4s. VO — none. Master track sits low and warm under the frame (subtle, never full).

DURATION: 6 seconds (the clip plays the full 6s at real-time natural speed).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, real-time playback at natural speed (no slow-motion), 180° shutter, natural motion blur.

LIP-SYNC: none — lips softly parted, composed, no words.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (vine/gown/hair), premature transform, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker, eye-colour drift.

## Frame 2 of 6 — IMAGE PROMPT (LIVING-VINE TOPIARY TRANSFORM)

IDENTITY LOCK: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here].

TRANSFORM KEYFRAME NOTE: START keyframe = the plain moss-green velvet column gown of Frame 1; END keyframe = a sculpted living-vine topiary couture gown — climbing vines, glossy emerald leaves and vivid pop-colour buds woven into a structured bodice and full leaf-tiered skirt. Lock identity, pose-continuity and the START/END silhouette so the growth reads as one continuous real-physics move; no second Aira, no teleport, no frame skip.

VISUAL-LEAD NOTE (silent reel): this is the showpiece transform — sell it on pure motion and colour: living vines racing up the gown, leaves unfurling in waves, electric buds swelling — mind-blowing growth carried entirely on image and sound, zero dialogue.

WARDROBE: (transforming) — the moss-velvet column is overtaken in a rising wave by living vines that weave a structured leaf-bodice and a full tiered skirt of overlapping glossy emerald leaves, threaded with swelling buds of vivid fuchsia, marigold, coral and electric-blue; fully modest high neckline preserved throughout; real botanical weight and drape, no floating leaves.

FOOTWEAR (transforming): the gold-leaf strappy heels stay, fine new tendrils spiralling up the ankle and lacing into living-vine anklets, tiny leaf-buds opening along the straps; real contact with the mossy stone, no mismatched footwear.

ACCESSORIES (transforming): the gold-leaf ear-climber sprouts a single living tendril curling along the ear, and the emerald-drop pendant is haloed by a tiny ring of opening leaflets; understated, catching crisp speculars, never competing with the bloom.

HAIR (transforming): the soft botanical updo gains fine living tendrils threading through, a few jewel-bright buds nesting at the crown; loose face-framing pieces lifting in the growth-draught; real strands, hair colour locked to the reference.

MAKEUP : the dewy garden-fresh glow holds, cheekbones catching the rising green-gold bounce, a fresh luminous sheen building as colour floods in around her; real skin with visible pores and peach-fuzz.

EYE COLOUR: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; pops of fuchsia and marigold reflecting as tiny coloured catchlights without changing iris colour; both irises matched, zero drift, no heterochromia.

HANDS & NAILS: right hand still cradling the emerald bottle, a vine curling gently around the wrist; left hand opening as leaves unfurl across the palm's air; almond nails in clean rose-nude gloss, neat cuticles, natural nail-bed colour.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: lips parting a few millimetres on a soft wondering breath, eyes widening a touch with delight as the colour blooms around her, brows lifting about 2mm, a smile beginning; vivid coloured catchlights dancing in the iris; alive and present (no speech).

BODY POSTURE & WEIGHT: a gentle rise and slow quarter-turn opening the new bodice to camera, arms easing outward as the skirt builds, weight shifting smoothly onto the front foot, spine lengthening; grounded, real momentum, mid-transformation.

KINETIC STILLNESS (8 layers): (1) vines racing visibly up the gown in a rising wave; (2) glossy leaves unfurling in sequence across the skirt; (3) vivid buds swelling and just beginning to split; (4) fine tendrils spiralling up the arms and hair; (5) a flurry of loosed pollen-light and tiny leaf-flecks lifting; (6) the emerald oil glinting as the wrist turns; (7) the velvet pile dissolving into leaf-texture along the transform line; (8) chest rising on the wondering inhale.

SPATIAL LOGIC: FOREGROUND — unfurling leaves and the cradled bottle crossing frame, sharp. MIDGROUND — Aira mid-transform, vines weaving the couture gown, the hero. BACKGROUND — the conservatory bursting into answering colour, topiary blooming, pollen-light thickening, deep green depth.

LIGHTING: KEY — the green-gold daylight lifting brighter as colour floods in. FILL — leaf-bounced green lifting shadows. RIM — warm sun-rim tracing the new leaf-silhouette. PRACTICAL — sun shafts intensifying through the glass. SEPARATION — a bright sunlit gap holding her edge against the busy bloom. BOUNCE — a card keeping a clean catch on the bottle and face.

FRAMING: ASPECT 9:16; easing from medium-close toward medium as the skirt builds, 10% headroom, the growth filling the lower two-thirds.
SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: A medium transformation showpiece, waist-up and easing wider as the look builds, about 10% headroom. Her body easing through the transform, weight rolling forward, torso opening toward the lens, the transform climbing the figure. Camera at mid distance easing back, clean negative space in the verdant conservatory. The frame reads from roughly the waist up, near-frontal three-quarter, widening to take in the building couture. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 40mm, f/2.5; face and weaving bodice sharp, the blooming conservatory to creamy multi-colour bokeh, vivid round speculars off dew and glass; clean highlight roll-off on the saturated colour, no clipping.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: a mind-blowing living-couture grow-on — vivid, kinetic, phone-stopping, the single impossible move of the reel building.

ATMOSPHERE: electric, lush, magical — a garden erupting into pop colour around a calm radiant figure.

COLOR GRADE: bright VIBRANT POP-COLOUR botanical — vivid emerald and moss with electric fuchsia, marigold, coral and electric-blue blossoms, gold-green daylight, dewy porcelain skin, high saturation kept clean and rich-but-open, no teal-orange, no muddy mids.

TEXTURE & MICRO-DETAIL: real leaf micro-texture — visible veins, glossy cuticle sheen, fine serrated edges; vine fibre and tiny thorns reading true; buds with dewed petal-skin just splitting; the velvet-to-leaf transition line crisp and physical; pollen-light reading as real fine grains, not a flat overlay.

SPOKEN LINE: NONE — silent transform; a soft wondering breath only, no speech.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, over-smoothed skin, oversharpened, AI artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, mismatched footwear, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, floating leaves, second subject, heterochromia, eye-colour drift, muddy colour.

## Frame 3 of 6 — IMAGE PROMPT (PRODUCT HERO)

IDENTITY LOCK: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here].

VISUAL-LEAD NOTE (silent reel): the product beauty beat — the emerald oil meeting the cheekbone in a luminous dewy glide, hero glass forward; sell the glow and the gesture on image, no dialogue.

WARDROBE: (resolved) — the living-vine topiary couture gown settled: a structured emerald leaf-bodice and tiered leaf-skirt threaded with vivid pop-colour buds, fully modest neckline, real botanical weight and a soft sway.

FOOTWEAR: the gold-leaf strappy heels with living-vine anklets, tiny leaf-buds open along the straps, soft specular on the gold; real contact, matched to the gown.

ACCESSORIES: the gold-leaf ear-climber with its curled tendril, the emerald-drop pendant haloed by tiny leaflets; one clean pin-specular each, understated next to the hero glass.

HAIR : the botanical updo with threaded tendrils and a couple of jewel-bright buds at the crown, a few soft face-framing pieces; real strands, hair colour locked to the reference.

MAKEUP : the dewy garden-fresh glow at full luminance, cheekbone lit where the oil meets skin, soft rosewood lip, fresh petal-pink blush; real skin with visible pores and peach-fuzz.

EYE COLOUR: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; crisp catchlights, a faint coloured bloom-reflection without changing iris colour; matched irises, zero drift, no heterochromia.

HANDS & NAILS: right hand bringing the open emerald bottle to the cheekbone, a single luminous green-gold oil-drop poised at the applicator; left hand resting softly at the collarbone; almond nails in clean rose-nude gloss, neat cuticles, natural nail-bed colour.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: eyes half-lowering toward the touch then lifting to lens, a serene satisfied micro-smile, lips softly closed, a gentle cheek-lift; warm catchlights crisp; calm and luminous (no speech).

BODY POSTURE & WEIGHT: a graceful slight lean toward the bottle, chin tipped a few degrees, near shoulder dropped, weight settled and grounded; intimate and poised.

KINETIC STILLNESS (8 layers): (1) the green-gold oil-drop swelling at the applicator tip; (2) a faint dewy sheen blooming where oil meets cheekbone; (3) a loose tendril easing at the temple; (4) a single bud behind softly finishing its open; (5) pollen-light drifting slow up-frame; (6) a travelling specular on the emerald glass; (7) chest settling on a calm breath; (8) a slow eyelash settle into the micro-smile.

SPATIAL LOGIC: FOREGROUND — the emerald bottle and oil-drop at the cheekbone, tack sharp, label forward. MIDGROUND — Aira's lit face and leaf-bodice, the hero. BACKGROUND — the blooming conservatory soft and creamy, pop-colour buds as bokeh.

LIGHTING: KEY — a soft green-gold beauty key shaping the cheek where oil meets skin. FILL — leaf-bounce green fill. RIM — warm sun-rim on hair and jaw. PRACTICAL — sun shafts behind. SEPARATION — a bright gap behind the head. BOUNCE — a card lifting a clean catch on the glass and the oil-drop.

FRAMING: ASPECT 9:16; beauty close, chest-up, 11% headroom, bottle and cheekbone on a strong third.
SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: A beauty close-up, chest-up, product-at-cheek hero with about 11% headroom, the bottle entering the lower third. Her body composed and near-frontal, the application hand raised to the cheekbone with soft wrist tension. Camera near at beauty distance, clean negative space, the verdant conservatory soft behind. Only head, shoulders and the raised hand are in frame — an intimate three-quarter product beat. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 85mm, f/2.0; eye, oil-drop and label tack sharp, the conservatory melting to creamy multi-colour bokeh, soft round speculars; clean roll-off.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: a luminous product-at-cheek beauty hero — dewy, premium, the glow the payoff.

ATMOSPHERE: intimate, fresh, radiant — the moment the botanical glow lands.

COLOR GRADE: bright VIBRANT POP-COLOUR botanical — vivid emerald with pop-colour bud bokeh, gold-green key, dewy porcelain skin, high-clean saturation, rich-but-open, no teal-orange.

TEXTURE & MICRO-DETAIL: the green-gold oil-drop reads with real viscosity and a sub-surface glow; dewy skin micro-texture with peach-fuzz catching the key; the emerald glass shows real frosted grain and a polished label window; leaf-bodice veins and cuticle sheen crisp; a faint oil-sheen spreading believably on the cheek.

SPOKEN LINE: NONE — silent beauty beat; a serene closed-lip micro-smile.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, over-smoothed skin, oversharpened, AI artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, mismatched footwear, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, garbled label text, heterochromia, eye-colour drift, muddy colour.

- [00:04–00:06] She lands exactly on the opening posture, framing and headroom matched, holding still for the seamless hand-back — a frame-accurate loop seam.

LIGHTING: the green-gold daylight easing back to the F1 direction and intensity, soft stone fill, warm sun-rim; steady, no flicker, matched to the opening.

ENVIRONMENT: the conservatory resolving to the calm opening look — topiary steadying, ferns settling, pollen-light thinning to the F1 drift.

AUDIO: diegetic-plus-design, no spoken word (silent reel). Ambient bed — the lush swell easing back down to the warm calm conservatory tone of the opening (birdsong, soft leaf-draught, low). SFX — a soft settling petal-flutter 0.0 to 1.8s, a gentle glass-settle as the bottle comes to rest at 2.4s, the airy shimmer thinning to silence by 4.8s for a clean loop point. Reaction — a soft quiet breath at 2.6s. VO — none. Master track resolves its phrase and eases to the low warm bed, landing soft so the loop back to Frame 1 is seamless (subtle, never full).

DURATION: 6 seconds (the clip plays the full 6s at real-time natural speed).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, real-time playback at natural speed (no slow-motion), 180° shutter, natural motion blur.

LIP-SYNC: none — a soft serene smile, lips just parted, no words.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (glow/leaf/petal), loop-mismatch, jarring cut, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker, eye-colour drift, muddy colour.

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key / Tempo: F♯ major, around 90 BPM — a fresh, unused key/tempo for this set; lush and verdant, lifting but never frantic.

Instrumentation: a lush botanical orchestral bed — warm legato strings, harp arpeggios, celesta sparkle, soft woodwinds (flute/clarinet) and a light glockenspiel, with a soft timpani roll reserved for the blossom-burst crest.

Arc: sits low and warm under F1–F4, lifts gently through the living-vine transform, rises to its fullest-but-still-restrained moment under the F5 blossom-burst, then resolves and eases back to the low warm bed under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: organic, dewy, verdant — airy and luminous, never dense; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the final phrase lands soft and open on F6 so the track restarts cleanly into F1 (perfect 30s loop).

# CONCEPT 72 — POP-ART COLOUR-BLOCK STUDIO / TERRAZZO-FORM COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 7 — Pop Graphic Maximalism

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Graphic Product Performance

Hero Product: "Prism Pop" multi-use cheek-and-lip tint — glossy clear-acrylic puck compact, candy-bright coral-to-magenta gel, chrome twist-lid

Setting: Pop-art colour-block studio — bold flat panels of primary yellow, cyan and magenta with hard graphic edges (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: colour-blocked structured mini-dress (cyan bodice, magenta peplum, yellow belt) with crisp graphic seams

Footwear: glossy magenta patent square-toe ankle boots, chrome block heel, clean unscuffed soles

Accessories: oversized yellow acrylic hoop earrings, one chunky cyan resin cuff, a chrome mini-ring stack

Hair : sleek high-shine graphic bob with a razor-blunt fringe, glassy finish, one bold travelling sheen band

Makeup : pop-graphic glow — glossy coral-magenta lip, diffused candy blush, clean glossy lids, inner-corner brightener

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating compact (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "pure colour, pure pop"

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: ELECTRIC · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, bold negative space, hard colour-block backdrop

Grade: hyper-vibrant pop-art — punchy saturated primaries, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, colour and light

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: B♭ minor, around 122 BPM — punchy, upbeat electro-pop-art energy, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a crisp synth-pop bed — bright plucky analog synth stabs, a tight punchy kick-and-clap groove, glossy arpeggiated synth, a clean sub-bass pulse, and a few candy bell-synth sparkles reserved for the halftone-dot burst crest.

Arc: sits tight and low under F1–F4 (groove present but restrained), lifts through the terrazzo-form energy, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled moment under the F5 dot-burst, then resolves and eases back to the low tight groove under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: glossy, graphic, electric — clean and punchy, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the final phrase lands tight and open on F6 so the track restarts cleanly into F1 (perfect 30s loop).

# CONCEPT 73 — TROPICAL NEON GARDEN / WOVEN-RATTAN COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 9 — Tropical Neon Maximalism

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Fragrance Performance

Hero Product: "Bloom Mist" hair-and-body fragrance — neon-clear faceted bottle, electric-green pump collar, luminous chartreuse-to-pink juice

Setting: Neon tropical-garden studio — oversized backlit monstera and palm silhouettes glowing hot-pink, electric-green and ultraviolet (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: sculptural woven-rattan bodice over a fluid electric-green slip dress, hot-pink piping along the weave

Footwear: strappy ultraviolet patent heeled sandals with a clear lucite block heel, clean soles

Accessories: oversized neon-green resin drop earrings, a woven-rattan cuff, a single hot-pink acrylic ring

Hair : high-gloss tropical wet-look waves swept to one side, deep side part, luminous sheen, zero flyaways

Makeup : neon-glow editorial — glossy hot-pink lip, dewy skin, a wash of electric-green shimmer on the inner lid, brightened inner corners

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating bottle (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "bloom in neon"

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: TROPICAL · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, glowing botanical backdrop, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant tropical neon — punchy chartreuse, hot-pink and ultraviolet, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, colour and glowing light

## Frame 1 of 6 — IMAGE PROMPT

## Frame 5 of 6 — VIDEO PROMPT

IDENTITY & CHARACTER-CONSISTENCY LOCK: render Aira strictly from the locked identity reference and hold her the SAME PERSON for the entire 6-second clip and every generated frame. Treat identity as a FIXED skeleton that never changes — bone structure (skull, cheekbones, jawline, chin), overall face shape and proportions, eye shape, spacing and iris colour, nose and lip shape, skin tone and real skin texture (visible pores, fine peach-fuzz; no plastic smoothing, no beautification creep, no face re-shaping), hairline, hair colour and texture, height, build and hand/finger anatomy. ABSOLUTE ZERO identity drift: no morphing, melting, smearing, rubbery warping, face-swapping, twinning or a second/duplicate subject, no age, weight, ethnicity or gender shift, no extra, missing or fused fingers or limbs. Identity stays identical at the first frame, every in-between frame, the loop seam and the last frame. Through any transform, impossible move or fast action ONLY the intended element (wardrobe, environment, props or effect) changes — her face, identity and proportions stay fully recognizable; interpolate strictly between the locked keyframes and never invent a new face, new hands, extra limbs or a second subject. ### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: C♯ minor, around 115 BPM — lush, sun-warmed tropical-house energy, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a glossy tropical-house bed — warm marimba and kalimba plucks, a soft deep-house kick and gentle shaker groove, mellow plucked synth, a round sub-bass pulse, and airy steel-pan and bell sparkles reserved for the orchid-bloom crest.

Arc: sits low and warm under F1–F4 (groove present but restrained), lifts through the woven-rattan energy, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled moment under the F5 orchid-bloom burst, then resolves and eases back to the low warm groove under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: glossy, sun-warmed, luminous — breezy and clean, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the final phrase lands soft and open on F6 so the track restarts cleanly into F1 (perfect 30s loop).

# CONCEPT 74 — PASTEL CHALK-ART STUDIO / CHALK-BLOOM COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 4 — Dreamy Pastel Maximalism

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Product Performance

Hero Product: "Sorbet Glow" pastel highlighter palette — clear-acrylic compact with a swirled rainbow-pastel pressed-powder dome, rose-chrome rim

Setting: Pastel chalk-art studio — a giant sugar-paper backdrop covered in vivid hand-drawn pastel chalk murals (mint, lilac, peach, sky-blue, butter-yellow), soft chalk-dust drifting in the air (hyper-vibrant pastel-pop)

Wardrobe: a structured pastel-ombré bodice over a full tiered tulle skirt graduating mint-to-lilac-to-peach, crisp graphic seams

Footwear: pastel-lilac patent slingback pumps with a clear lucite heel, soft pearl buckle, clean unscuffed soles

Accessories: oversized pastel-swirl resin hoop earrings, a chunky mint resin cuff, a single peach acrylic ring

Hair : sleek high-shine pastel-dipped low chignon with a glossy finish and a soft lilac-to-peach ombré on the loose face-framing pieces, zero flyaways

Makeup : pastel-pop glow — glossy sorbet-peach lip, dewy skin, a wash of pastel-lilac shimmer on the lid, soft pink blush, brightened inner corners

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating palette (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "drawn in light"

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: DREAMY · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, soft pastel chalk-mural backdrop, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant pastel-pop — punchy mint, lilac, peach, sky-blue and butter-yellow, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy or chalky-grey

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, pastel colour and soft light

Tonal-lane note: soft dreamy pastel-pop lane — a gentle airy departure from C71's deep botanical, C72's hard primary pop-art and C73's electric tropical neon, while staying vivid and never muddy

ABSOLUTE ZERO identity drift: no morphing, melting, smearing, rubbery warping, face-swapping, twinning or a second/duplicate subject, no age, weight, ethnicity or gender shift, no extra, missing or fused fingers or limbs. Identity stays identical at the first frame, every in-between frame, the loop seam and the last frame. ### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: A♭ major, around 100 BPM — a soft dreamy pastel-pop bed, airy and sweet, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a gentle pastel-pop bed — soft felt-piano and music-box bells, a mellow pluck synth, a light brushed-kick and finger-snap groove, warm pad swells, and a delicate harp-glissando and chime-sparkle reserved for the rainbow-bloom crest.

Arc: opens soft and dreamy under F1–F3 (gentle groove, breathing room), warms through the chalk-bloom transform, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled shimmer under the F5 rainbow-bloom burst, then resolves and eases back to the soft dreamy bed under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: airy, sweet, luminous — soft and clean like sugar-paper and pastel light, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the closing music-box phrase resolves gently on F6 and leaves an open, unresolved-sweet tail so the pastel-pop bed slips seamlessly back into the F1 felt-piano opening (perfect 30-second loop).

# CONCEPT 75 — ELECTRIC POP-CITRUS STUDIO / SEQUIN-CASCADE COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 8 — Hyper-Glam Pop

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Product Performance

Hero Product: "Citrus Flash" vitamin-C glow drops — faceted citrine-glass dropper bottle, electric-orange cap, glowing amber-gold liquid

Setting: Electric citrus-pop studio — suspended glossy citrus slices (orange, lime, lemon) and frozen juice-splash colour arcs against a hot citrus-coral cyclorama (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: a liquid-sequin mini-gown with structured shoulders and a sharp hem, the sequins colour-flipping electric-orange to magenta to lime as light moves

Footwear: electric-orange patent platform heels with a clear PVC counter, pristine unscuffed soles

Accessories: oversized lime-green resin hoop earrings, a stack of citrus-toned bangles on the left wrist, a faceted citrine cocktail ring

Hair : a sleek high-shine deep-side-part bob with a wet-look finish and an electric-orange tip-flash on the longer side, razor-clean hairline, zero flyaways

Makeup : citrus-pop glow — glossy tangerine lip, dewy glass skin, an electric-lime inner-corner pop, golden high-shine highlight on the cheekbone and brow-bone

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating bottle (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "switch on the glow"

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: ELECTRIC · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, suspended citrus and juice-arc backdrop, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant pop-citrus — punchy electric-orange, lime, lemon-yellow, magenta and citrus-coral, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, electric citrus colour and high-gloss light

Tonal-lane note: high-energy electric-citrus glam lane — a punchy departure from C71's botanical, C72's hard primary pop-art, C73's tropical neon and C74's soft pastel, while staying vivid and never muddy

External master reaches its fullest-but-still-controlled crest here, then begins easing.

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: E major, around 126 BPM — a bright electro-disco-pop bed, punchy and effervescent, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a glossy electro-disco bed — a tight four-on-the-floor kick and crisp hi-hats, a funky filtered disco-bass, plucky synth stabs, a bright arpeggiated lead, and a shimmer-riser and white-noise sweep reserved for the supernova crest.

Arc: sits tight and bright under F1–F4 (groove driving but controlled), surges through the sequin-cascade energy, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled lift under the F5 supernova burst, then resolves and eases back to the tight bright groove under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: glossy, effervescent, electric — punchy and clean, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the closing arpeggio lands clean on the downbeat of F6 and leaves a bright open synth-tail so the disco-pop groove snaps seamlessly back into the F1 kick (perfect 30-second loop).

# CONCEPT 76 — ULTRAVIOLET GLOSS-DRIP STUDIO / LIQUID-ENAMEL POUR COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 6 — High-Gloss Futurism

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Product Performance

Hero Product: "Vinyl Shine" liquid lip lacquer — a sleek chrome-capped glass vial of mirror-gloss lacquer, electric-violet liquid

Setting: Ultraviolet gloss studio — glossy enamel paint-drip walls in electric jewel tones over a mirror-reflective floor, UV-bright (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: a high-gloss liquid-vinyl gown that reads wet-painted, an electric-blue-to-ultraviolet ombré with a sculptural peplum and a sharp hem

Footwear: ultraviolet patent knee boots in mirror-gloss with a sculpted heel, pristine unscuffed soles

Accessories: a chrome-and-fuchsia statement cuff, mirror-disc drop earrings, an electric-blue resin ring

Hair : a sleek wet-look sculpted finger-wave with an ultraviolet glaze riding the surface, razor-clean hairline, zero flyaways

Makeup : high-gloss jewel pop — mirror-gloss electric-violet lip, glassy skin, a foiled emerald lid accent, chrome highlight on the cheekbone and brow-bone

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating vial (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "wet to the touch"

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: SLEEK · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, jewel-tone gloss-drip backdrop, mirror floor, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant high-gloss jewel — punchy electric-blue, ultraviolet, fuchsia and emerald, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, electric jewel colour and high-gloss reflection

Tonal-lane note: sleek high-gloss jewel-futurism lane — a cool glossy departure from C71's botanical, C72's primary pop-art, C73's tropical neon, C74's soft pastel and C75's warm citrus, while staying vivid and never muddy

## Frame 6 of 6 — VIDEO PROMPT

Do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

External master resolves cool and open, easing back so the track restarts cleanly into Frame 1.

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: D minor, around 108 BPM — a sleek dark electro / future-bass bed, glossy and propulsive, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a polished future-bass bed — a deep round sub-bass, a punchy gated kick and tight rim-clicks, a glossy detuned supersaw swell, icy bell-plucks, and a filtered riser and reverse-cymbal reserved for the splash-crown crest.

Arc: sits dark and glossy under F1–F4 (groove restrained and cool), surges through the enamel-pour energy, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled lift under the F5 splash-crown burst, then resolves and eases back to the dark glossy groove under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: sleek, glossy, futuristic — cool and clean, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the closing sub-bass note decays smooth on F6 and leaves a cool open reverb-tail so the future-bass groove glides seamlessly back into the F1 sub pulse (perfect 30-second loop).

# CONCEPT 77 — PAPER-BLOOM GARDEN STUDIO / KIRIGAMI LACE-CUT COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 3 — Tactile Craft Maximalism

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Product Performance

Hero Product: "Petal Veil" silk setting powder — a round blush-coral compact with an embossed petal lid and a soft-focus pressed-powder dome

Setting: Paper-bloom garden studio — a backdrop of giant hand-cut kirigami paper flowers in hot-coral, marigold, fuchsia and turquoise over a layered paper-petal floor (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: a sculptural lace-cut paper gown of intricate kirigami petal layers in a coral-to-fuchsia graduation, a structured bodice and a voluminous petal skirt

Footwear: marigold-yellow satin pumps with a paper-petal ankle detail, pristine clean soles

Accessories: oversized turquoise paper-flower earrings, a coral lacquer cuff, a fuchsia statement ring

Hair : a sculpted glossy updo wrapped with a single kirigami paper-petal accent, razor-clean hairline, zero flyaways

Makeup : petal-pop glow — satin coral lip, dewy skin, soft fuchsia blush draped high, a gold-leaf inner-corner fleck

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating compact (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "unfold in bloom"

Duration: 30 seconds | 6 frames

Mood: JOYFUL · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, giant kirigami paper-flower backdrop, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant paper-bloom — punchy hot-coral, marigold, fuchsia and turquoise, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, vivid paper colour and soft craft-light

Tonal-lane note: joyful tactile paper-craft lane — a handmade departure from C71's living botanical, C72's primary pop-art, C73's tropical neon, C74's soft pastel, C75's warm citrus and C76's cool gloss, while staying vivid and never muddy

Keep expression changes smooth and moderate and lead them with the EYES and GAZE (soft smiles, brow lifts, a parted breath, eyes tracing the object) — no extreme grimace, no wide-mouth distortion, no hard squint, no rapid expression flicker that would warp the geometry; favour one clean expression transition per clip. ABSOLUTE ZERO identity drift: no morphing, melting, smearing, rubbery warping, face-swapping, twinning or a second/duplicate subject, no age, weight, ethnicity or gender shift, no extra, missing or fused fingers or limbs. Identity stays identical at the first frame, every in-between frame, the loop seam and the last frame. Through any transform, impossible move or fast action ONLY the intended element (wardrobe, environment, props or effect) changes — her face, identity and proportions stay fully recognizable; interpolate strictly between the locked keyframes and never invent a new face, new hands, extra limbs or a second subject. Do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

SHOT TYPE: medium close, chest-up, subject fills 55% of the vertical frame (matched to Frame 1).

CAMERA MOVEMENT: a gentle 6% settle-back that returns the framing to the Frame 1 start position (single move), no cut, no whip — engineered for a seamless loop.

LENS: 50mm, f/2.8.

SUBJECT ACTION WITH TIMING:
- 0.0–3.0s — the last paper-flecks settle as Aira eases her arms back in and re-cradles the petal compact at collarbone height.
- 3.0–6.0s — she resolves into the calm hero pose with the warm quarter-smile and a soft settling exhale, gaze direct to lens — the final composition matching Frame 1 exactly so the reel loops cleanly into the top.

LIGHTING: beauty key with clamshell fill (matched to Frame 1); soft speculars settling on the compact lid; hair-light steady; paper-flower wall one stop down.

ENVIRONMENT: paper-bloom garden studio, last paper-flecks fading, calm restored.

AUDIO: fully silent reel — no spoken word, no in-clip music. Diegetic and design only: room-tone bed easing back to the calm opening level; a soft compact-click as fingers re-settle on the lid near 3.6s (gentle, short tail, mirroring Frame 1's click); a faint paper-flex settle near 2.4s; a soft settling breath near 4.8s; a last delicate petal-fade near 1.2s. External master resolves warm and open, easing back so the track restarts cleanly into Frame 1.

DURATION: 5 seconds (0:25 to 0:30 of 30s total).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, 180° shutter, natural settle blur; playback 24fps real-time.

LIP-SYNC: none — calm quarter-smile, no words.

NEGATIVE: morphing, identity drift, loop-mismatch to Frame 1, abrupt cut, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, audio desync, wardrobe drift, unmotivated shake, physics violation (paper/hair), mannequin posture, frozen background, torn paper, heterochromia, eye-colour drift, muddy colour.

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: A major, around 112 BPM — a bright handmade folk-pop bed, sunny and bouncy, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a warm folk-pop bed — a softly strummed ukulele, plucked nylon-string guitar, light hand-claps and finger-snaps, a gentle shaker and tambourine, soft glockenspiel sparkle, and a warm upright-bass pulse; a bright mallet-roll reserved for the bloom-burst crest.

Arc: sits warm and gentle under F1–F4 (strum light and intimate), lifts through the paper-fold energy, rises to its sunniest fullest-but-still-controlled lift under the F5 bloom-burst, then resolves and eases back to the gentle strum under F6 for a seamless loop.

Texture: sunny, handmade, organic — warm and clean, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the closing ukulele strum rings open on F6 and leaves a warm soft tail so the folk-pop groove drifts seamlessly back into the F1 opening strum (perfect 30-second loop).

# CONCEPT 78 — CANDY-CHROME BALLOON STUDIO / MYLAR-FOIL BALLOON COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 11 — Surreal Pop Art

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Product Performance

Hero Product: "Bubble Gloss" plumping lip gloss — a rounded bubble-shaped clear vial with a candy-pink dome cap and glossy bubblegum-pink liquid

Setting: Candy-chrome balloon studio — a backdrop of giant glossy chrome and candy-coloured mylar balloons (magenta, electric-cyan, lime, tangerine) over a glossy mirror-reflective floor (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: a sculptural mylar-foil balloon gown of inflated chrome-and-candy segments, glossy and reflective, a bubble-sculpted bodice and a rounded voluminous skirt

Footwear: chrome bubble-platform heels in mirror-finish with candy-pink soles, pristine

Accessories: oversized chrome heart-balloon earrings, an electric-cyan inflatable-look cuff, a candy-pink chrome ring

Hair : a sculpted glossy high bubble-bun wrapped with a chrome ribbon, razor-clean hairline, zero flyaways

Makeup : candy-gloss pop — high-shine bubblegum-pink lip, glassy skin, a glossy magenta-to-cyan gradient lid, chrome highlight

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating bubble-vial (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "blow it up"

Duration: 30 seconds | 8 frames

Mood: PLAYFUL · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centered hero, giant chrome-and-candy balloon backdrop, glossy floor, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant candy-chrome — punchy magenta, electric-cyan, lime and tangerine with mirror-chrome accents, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, candy colour and glossy chrome reflection

Tonal-lane note: playful surreal candy-pop lane — a bouncy chrome-balloon departure from C71's botanical, C72's primary pop-art, C73's tropical neon, C74's pastel, C75's citrus, C76's cool gloss and C77's paper-craft, while staying vivid and never muddy

## Frame 7 of 8 — VIDEO PROMPT (POST-BURST FLOAT)

IDENTITY & CHARACTER-CONSISTENCY LOCK: render Aira strictly from the locked identity reference and hold her the SAME PERSON for the entire 6-second clip and every generated frame. Treat identity as a FIXED skeleton that never changes — bone structure (skull, cheekbones, jawline, chin), overall face shape and proportions, eye shape, spacing and iris colour, nose and lip shape, skin tone and real skin texture (visible pores, fine peach-fuzz; no plastic smoothing, no beautification creep, no face re-shaping), hairline, hair colour and texture, height, build and hand/finger anatomy. ONLY the soft expression muscles may move — eyelids, brows, cheeks and mouth corners — together with the eyes, gaze and head; expression and lip-sync animate ON TOP of that fixed identity and must NEVER alter the face shape, the eye colour, or who she is. Keep expression changes smooth and moderate and lead them with the EYES and GAZE (soft smiles, brow lifts, a parted breath, eyes tracing the object) — no extreme grimace, no wide-mouth distortion, no hard squint, no rapid expression flicker that would warp the geometry; favour one clean expression transition per clip. ABSOLUTE ZERO identity drift: no morphing, melting, smearing, rubbery warping, face-swapping, twinning or a second/duplicate subject, no age, weight, ethnicity or gender shift, no extra, missing or fused fingers or limbs. Identity stays identical at the first frame, every in-between frame, the loop seam and the last frame. Through any transform, impossible move or fast action ONLY the intended element (wardrobe, environment, props or effect) changes — her face, identity and proportions stay fully recognizable; interpolate strictly between the locked keyframes and never invent a new face, new hands, extra limbs or a second subject. Do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

SHOT TYPE: medium-full, slightly low, settling hero.

CAMERA MOVEMENT: a gentle 5% ease-down settling from the burst rise; one smooth move, no cut, no whip.

LENS: 40mm, f/2.2.

SUBJECT ACTION WITH TIMING:
- 0.0–3.0s — the confetti supernova eases to a soft drifting halo as Aira lowers her arms and her serene smile settles.
- 3.0–6.0s — she eases toward a calm upright hero stance, confetti drifting past, holding luminous and composed. One clean settling action, real physics.

LIGHTING: studio beauty light easing back, warm rim holding her in the thinning sparkle, soft confetti bounce; steady, no flicker.

ENVIRONMENT: the studio calming, last balloons spent, chrome glitter thinning, glossy mirror-floor doubling the soft sparkle.

AUDIO: fully silent reel — no spoken word, no in-clip music. Diegetic and design only: room-tone bed; a soft confetti-flutter settle 0.0 to 3.0s; a gentle chrome-shimmer thinning to near-silence by 5.0s; a soft calm breath near 3.6s. External master eases down from the burst toward its calm bed.

DURATION: 3 seconds (0:24 to 0:27 of 30s total).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, 180° shutter, gentle natural motion blur on the settle; playback 24fps real-time.

LIP-SYNC: none — a serene settling smile, no words.

NEGATIVE: morphing, identity drift, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, audio desync, unmotivated shake, physics violation (confetti/hair/mylar), mannequin posture, frozen background, dented mylar, heterochromia, eye-colour drift, muddy colour.

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: E♭ major, around 120 BPM — a fresh, unused key/tempo for this set; bouncy, candy electro-pop, playful and buoyant, never frantic.

Instrumentation: a bright candy electro-pop bed — plucky synth bass, a bouncy four-on-the-floor kick with hand-claps, glossy marimba-synth and bell plucks, a shimmer of vocoder-free pad, with a bright riser and a soft confetti-glitter sparkle reserved for the F6 balloon-burst supernova.

Arc: sits low and bouncy under F1–F5 (groove present but restrained), lifts through the mylar inflate-form, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled moment under the F6 balloon-burst supernova, eases through the F7 afterglow, then resolves back to the low bouncy bed under F8 for a seamless loop.

Texture: glossy, candy-bright, buoyant — clean and poppy, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the closing synth-bass note pops soft and round on F8 and leaves a light candy-bright tail so the bouncy electro-pop groove springs seamlessly back into the F1 opening pluck (perfect 30-second loop).

# CONCEPT 79 — PRISM MIRROR STUDIO / IRIDESCENT OIL-SLICK HOLOGRAPHIC COUTURE (SILENT)

Title: Pillar 1 — Futuristic Iridescent Chrome

Format: Commercial Beauty Hero / Holographic Product Performance

Hero Product: "Prism Drops" iridescent liquid highlighter — a faceted prism-cut clear-glass bottle, holographic chrome dropper cap, pearlescent rainbow-shifting liquid

Setting: Mirror-prism studio — chrome-mirror panels and hanging cut-glass prisms throwing full-spectrum rainbow refractions, clean prismatic light-beams crossing the air (hyper-vibrant)

Wardrobe: sculptural faceted holographic prism gown of iridescent rainbow-shifting mirror-foil panels over a liquid-chrome bodysuit

Footwear: clear lucite prism-heel sandals with holographic iridescent straps and a chrome platform, clean unscuffed soles

Accessories: faceted prism-drop earrings, a liquid-chrome cuff, one holographic iridescent ring

Hair: sleek high-shine chrome-glass waves with an iridescent holographic sheen, deep side part, zero flyaways

Makeup: holographic glass-glow — iridescent pearl highlight, glossy prism-shift lip, crystalline inner-corner brighten, dewy skin

Eye Colour: locked to the Aira reference — warm hazel-brown with a soft amber inner ring; zero drift, both irises matched, no heterochromia

Movement: macro rack-focus then a graphic 3D orbit on the levitating prism bottle (beauty mandate)

Concept Line (NOT spoken): "split the light"

Duration: 30 seconds | 7 frames

Mood: IRIDESCENT · VIBRANT · MIND-BLOWING

Composition: centred hero, mirror-prism depth, clean negative space

Grade: hyper-vibrant holographic prism — full-spectrum iridescent rainbow over chrome, crisp whites, rich uncrushed blacks, full mid-tone, zero grain, never muddy

Spoken line: NONE (fully silent — no VO any frame)

Audio note: per-frame diegetic SFX plus design only; separate Master Track Brief after the final frame; subtle, never full

Identity safety: adult, non-sexualized; face, bone structure and hair locked to the reference; zero drift

Visual-lead note: every beat reads in absolute silence through motion, refracted colour and prismatic light

Tonal-lane note: bright futuristic holographic/chrome lane — a fresh iridescent departure from the candy-balloon, botanical and pop-art lanes earlier in the set

### 🎵 Master Track Brief (External Audio Layer)

Key & Tempo: E♭ major, around 120 BPM — a bouncy, candy electro-pop bounce, distinct from every other concept's track.

Instrumentation: a glossy candy electro-pop bed — bouncy plucked synth-bass, a tight punchy kick-and-clap groove, bright marimba-synth and bubblegum bell plinks, a glassy arpeggiated synth, with a sparkling riser and a soft chime-shimmer reserved for the balloon-burst supernova crest.

Arc: sits tight and low under F1–F5 (bounce present but restrained), lifts through the mylar-inflate transform, rises to its fullest-but-still-controlled moment under the F6 balloon-burst supernova, eases through the F7 afterglow, then resolves and settles back to the low bouncy bed under F8 for a seamless loop.

Texture: glossy, bouncy, candy-bright — clean and effervescent, never dense or muddy; an external layer that supports the silent reel without ever stepping on the designed diegetic sound.

Mix rule: present but always background — ducks under every SFX and breath; no melodic vocal, no lyrics, no spoken word anywhere (fully silent reel).

Loop: the bouncy synth-bass figure lands light and open as the closing chime-shimmer fades on F8, so the candy electro-pop groove springs cleanly back into the F1 opening pluck (perfect 30-second loop)..4 to 1.6s — the burst races outward balloon to balloon as foil-shards, candy confetti and chrome glitter lift and swirl around her, she lifting her eyes into the swirl; 1.6 to 3.0s — the confetti trails out, easing to a sustained drifting halo, her radiant smile landing; 3.0 to 4.0s — she holds, haloed and triumphant. Only the synchronized balloon-burst is impossible; all else real physics.

LIGHTING: the burst lifted as a live key over the studio beauty light, bright rim, confetti-and-foil fill rising; controlled, no clipping.

ENVIRONMENT: studio alive with bursting chrome-and-candy balloons, chrome glitter streaming, swirling and trailing confetti, glossy mirror-floor doubling the spectacle.

AUDIO: fully silent reel — no spoken word, no in-clip music. Diegetic and design only: room-tone bed blooming into a lush designed swell cresting at the burst then settling. SFX — a soft balloon-swell creak 0.2s, a synchronized cluster of soft mylar-pops and an airy confetti-spray tracking the swirl 0.4 to 1.6s, soft foil-flutter and confetti settling 1.2 to 2.8s, a warm resonance under the settle. Reaction — a soft powerful breath at 1.4s. External master rises to its fullest-but-still-restrained moment under the burst then eases (subtle, never full).

DURATION: 4 seconds (0:20 to 0:24 of 30s total).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, 180° shutter, natural motion blur on the burst and swirling confetti; playback 24fps real-time.
